## Qulla + N=1 trailing-limit, NO time stop — monthly breakdown (min-bucket half-Kelly sized) — 2026-06-17

**This is the new default system from 2026-06-17 onward** (supersedes the V1-exit system above for the headline). Same 5-filter final system (entry≥$5, within 5% of the 52w-high close — the **0.95 band**, breadth>0.5 [pct_above_20, lagged 1d], RVOL 6–20, tightness<0.30, **ATR%<8%**), but with the **Qullamaggie entry-day-low stop + N=1 mean-reversion trailing limit + 0.70 expansion exit, no time stop**. **3,671 trips.** Sized by the **min(breadth_tercile, rvol_tercile) half-Kelly** weights **recomputed on THIS system's realized returns** — bucket PFs 2.07 / 2.75 / 3.18 → half-Kelly **0.113 / 0.153 / 0.166** (normalized to mean weight 1 ⇒ per-bucket weights 0.85× / 1.16× / 1.25×; pure reallocation, no added leverage). These are *higher* than the old system's 0.074/0.108/0.176 because the no-time-stop + N=1 exit lifts PF in every bucket.

Total net P&L **+$1,799,216** (Kelly-sized) vs flat-$10k **+$1,715,972**. P&L bucketed by **exit** date (realized P&L lands when the trade closes). **PF and net P&L are Kelly-weighted; win% is unweighted (per-trade).**

> **⚠️ Small-n PF caveat:** at monthly granularity many months have only 1–8 trades, so the monthly **PF column is noisy** — a single win with no losses shows `inf`, and one loss can crater it. **Trust the net P&L sign and win% for the monthly read; PF is only meaningful at the yearly / bucket level** (large n).

### Headline

- **Months in profit: 169/248 = 68.1%** (full history 2005-02 → 2026-05). *Comfortably clears the >60% target.*
- **Years in profit: 21/22** — only **2025 negative** (−$2,292, marginal).
- **Asymmetry: avg positive month +$11,966 vs avg negative month −$2,905** (≈4:1) — the engine of the edge.
- **Worst single month: 2025-07 −$19,034.** Best: 2021-01 +$285,534.
- **Max drawdown on monthly realized equity: −$48,907** (trough 2025-09).
- **Worst losing streak: 6 consecutive months (2025-01 … 2025-07, cumulative −$43,967).** Next worst: 5 months (2022-08 … 2023-01). Streak-length distribution: 1mo×33, 2mo×11, 3mo×3, 4mo×1, 5mo×1, 6mo×1.
- **2025 is the lone weak year** (PF 0.98) — concentrated in 2025-02/05/07/09 (the 6-month streak). Flagged for investigation (regime? a specific blow-up cluster?).

## Trailing-stop window sweep — full monthly/yearly breakdowns, all 14 windows (2026-06-17)

The [stop-window sweep](momentum_v0_results.md#trailing-stop-window-sweep--tighten-to-4-day-low-2026-06-17) showed PF rising and P&L plateauing-then-falling as `--stop-low-window` tightens from 14→1 on the Qulla N=1 no-time-stop default (same 3,671 entries each row; the window changes only *exits*). This is the **swing-vs-position knob**: a loose stop (14d) is position-trading, a 1d stop is Lance-Breitstein-style swing-trading. Below are the **consistency metrics and full breakdowns for every window**, each with half-Kelly sizing whose **bucket fractions are recomputed on that window's own realized returns**.

**The reader's takeaway:** as the stop tightens, **raw P&L falls but consistency rises dramatically** — months-profitable 69%→85%, max drawdown −$45k→−$3.3k (a ~14× reduction), every window 22/22 years positive from w≤9. **w=4 ⭐ is the P&L-on-plateau sweet spot; w=1 🛡 is the max-consistency / small-account / swing config** (give up ~40% P&L for a 14× smaller worst drawdown).
